This file is validated by the CI workflow at .github/workflows/codeowners-validator.yml, which runs mszostok/codeowners-validator with checks for files, duplicate patterns, and syntax validation.\\n\\nThe Go integration begins in pkg/services/featuremgmt/codeowners.go, which defines a codeowner type and constants for team ownership references (e.g., @grafana/grafana-app-platform-squad). These codeowners are assigned to feature flags in pkg/services/featuremgmt/registry.go, where each feature toggle includes an Owner field of type codeowner.\\n\\nManifest generation is orchestrated through pkg/services/featuremgmt/toggles_gen_test.go, which runs test cases that generate three key files: toggles_gen.go (Go backend), toggles_gen.csv (CSV data export), and toggles_gen.json (JSON manifest containing codeowner metadata). These generated files embed feature flag metadata including the codeowner field for programmatic access.\\n\\nThe frontend system is defined in pkg/apis/featuretoggle/v0alpha1/types.go, a Kubernetes-style API that includes FeatureSpec with an Owner field (JSON-keyed as codeowner) and auto-generated OpenAPI schemas in zz_generated.openapi.go. The TypeScript frontend types are generated in packages/grafana-data/src/types/featureToggles.gen.ts.\\n\\nThe JavaScript layer leverages the codeowners npm package (version ^5.1.1 in package.json) in scripts/cli/generateBettererIssues.ts, which parses the CODEOWNERS file and assigns code quality issues to team owners. The npm script betterer:issues invokes this TypeScript script to generate ownership-based issue reports.\\n\\nDocumentation integration is present in contribute/feature-toggles.md (contributor guide referencing CODEOWNERS), and docs/sources/setup-grafana/configure-grafana/feature-toggles/index.md (auto-generated feature toggle documentation).\\n\\nThis infrastructure creates a closed-loop system where CODEOWNERS definitions inform feature flag ownership, enable automated issue assignment, and generate manifests that propagate ownership metadata across backend, frontend, and CI/CD systems.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":12,"cache_creation_input_tokens":2688,"cache_read_input_tokens":80155,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":2688},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"2fbf2a91-a9a7-45a5-bf50-09a29c3935dc","uuid":"089fe65a-4eb9-4cc4-b334-e2867570ef13"}
